class="article-content__articleDetailCon__kmMNZ" id="617700"><div class="article-content__contextC__QMEJJ"><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 16px; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">最近如果你有在看美股<a href="https://www.mitrade.com/zh/insights/tag/tech-stocks" target="_blank">科技股</a>，很容易注意到一檔股票——<strong>SNDK（SanDisk）</strong>。從 2025年2月獨立上市以來，股價從不到<strong>30 美元</strong>一路飆到 <strong>850 美元</strong>以上，一年漲幅超過<strong>2600%</strong>，4月即將納入納斯達克100指數。</p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 16px; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">市場上到處都是關於SNDK的疑問：</p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 16px; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">👉 SNDK是做什麼的？跟AI有什麼關係？</p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 16px; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">👉 為什麼股價能暴漲這麼多，又經常大起大落？</p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 16px; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">這篇文章我會用一個比較實際的方式，幫你把SNDK拆解清楚，不僅告訴你公司在賺什麼錢、股價為什麼波動，更重要的是，幫你建立一套屬於自己的投資判斷標準，讓你看懂這檔股票的投資邏輯。</p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.714; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><br></p></div></div><div class="article-content__articleDetailCon__kmMNZ" id="617701"><div class="article-content__conP__unsXk"><div class="article-content__titleSerial__NBTps observe-item"></div><h2 class="article-content__contextP__E5lG3">SNDK是做什麼的？</h2></div><div class="article-content__contextC__QMEJJ"><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;"><strong>Sandisk Corporation（SNDK）</strong>是一家專注於「<strong>資料儲存</strong>」的半導體公司，核心技術是<strong> NAND Flash</strong>（快閃記憶體），簡單來說，就是負責製造「<strong>電子儲存空間</strong>」的公司。</p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">白話解釋一下，你每天用的手機記憶卡、筆電裡的 SSD 固態硬碟、USB 隨身碟，還有雲端資料中心裡用來儲存大量數據的設備，很多都是用 SanDisk 的 NAND Flash 技術製造的。你可以把它想成是數位世界的「倉庫管理員」，負責把所有數據妥善儲存起來，需要的時候再快速取出。</p><h3 style="padding: 0px; margin: 1.31249em 0px 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 1.142em; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); scroll-margin-top: 48px; white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">SNDK的三大市場</h3><h3 style="padding: 0px; margin: 1.31249em 0px 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 1.142em; line-height: 1.5; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); scroll-margin-top: 48px; white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><p style="position: absolute; margin-left: 6px; opacity: 0; transition: opacity 0.2s; line-height: 1.75em;"><span class="_1e0c1o8l _vchhusvi _1o9zidpf _vwz4kb7n _y4ti1igz _bozg1mb9 _12va1onz _jcxd1r8n" style="display: inline-block; flex-shrink: 0; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1; padding-inline: 0px; color: rgb(80, 82, 88);"></span></p></h3><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">根據 SanDisk 2026 財年 Q2 的財報數據，公司業務可以清晰拆成三個部分，每個部分的增長動力和利潤率都不一樣：</p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">1️⃣ <strong>消費電子</strong>：手機、電腦、數位相機等，這是 SanDisk 的傳統強項，也是大家最熟悉的業務。比如手機裡的內置儲存、替換用的記憶卡，筆電的 SSD 硬碟等，屬於穩定現金流業務，利潤率中等。</p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">2️⃣ <strong>企業/資料中心</strong>：雲端服務、AI 伺服器。這是2026年增長最快的業務，也是 SNDK 跟 AI 最直接相關的部分。AI 大模型訓練需要處理 PB 級的數據，一臺AI 伺服器對 NAND 儲存的需求是傳統伺服器的 3-8 倍，這種爆發性需求直接推動了公司業績增長。</p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">3️⃣ <strong>工業與車用</strong>：自動駕駛、邊緣運算設備的儲存需求。這部分業務規模相對小，但增長穩定。</p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">👉 <span style="color: rgb(0, 112, 192);">SNDK 本質上是「AI 時代的基礎設施供應商」。</span>AI 需要大量算力，更需要大量儲存空間，沒有足夠的 NAND Flash，再強大的 AI 模型也無法運轉。這也是為什麼 SNDK能在 AI浪潮中脫穎而出的關鍵原因。</p><h3 style="padding: 0px; margin: 1.31249em 0px 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 1.142em; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); scroll-margin-top: 48px; white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">為什麼SNDK會重新上市？</h3><h3 style="padding: 0px; margin: 1.31249em 0px 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 1.142em; line-height: 1.5; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); scroll-margin-top: 48px; white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><p style="position: absolute; margin-left: 6px; opacity: 0; transition: opacity 0.2s; line-height: 1.75em;"><span class="_1e0c1o8l _vchhusvi _1o9zidpf _vwz4kb7n _y4ti1igz _bozg1mb9 _12va1onz _jcxd1r8n" style="display: inline-block; flex-shrink: 0; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1; padding-inline: 0px; color: rgb(80, 82, 88);"></span></p></h3><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">很多人不知道，SanDisk 原本是 <strong>Western Digital（WDC</strong>，西部數據）的子公司，2025 年 2 月 21 日才正式<strong>拆分獨立上市</strong>，在納斯達克掛牌交易，股票代碼 SNDK。</p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">這件事看起來只是公司架構調整，實際上對投資人來說非常重要。因為<strong>拆分後，市場可以「單獨評價記憶體業務」</strong>。過去Sandisk夾在WDC內部，投資人很難直接對NAND Flash業務定價。拆分獨立之後，Sandisk的價值被重新發現，加上AI需求爆發，股價從拆分時的約27.89美元一路暴漲。</p><p style="line-height: 1.75em;"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); color: rgb(75, 75, 75); font-family: khula, source-han-sans-korean, open-sans, source-sans-pro, roboto, &quot;PingFang TC&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;"><br></span></p><h3 style="line-height: 1.75em;"><span id="617702"><div class="article-content__conP__unsXk"><div class="article-content__titleSerial__NBTps observe-item"></div><h2 class="article-content__contextP__E5lG3">SNDK股價為什麼波動這麼大？</h2></div><div class="article-content__contextC__QMEJJ"><h3 style="padding: 0px; margin: 1.31249em 0px 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 1.142em; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); scroll-margin-top: 48px; white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;"><span style="color: rgb(151, 72, 6);">記憶體產業是「強周期股」</span></h3><h3 style="padding: 0px; margin: 1.31249em 0px 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 1.142em; line-height: 1.5; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); scroll-margin-top: 48px; white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><p style="position: absolute; margin-left: 6px; opacity: 0; transition: opacity 0.2s; line-height: 1.75em;"><span class="_1e0c1o8l _vchhusvi _1o9zidpf _vwz4kb7n _y4ti1igz _bozg1mb9 _12va1onz _jcxd1r8n" style="display: inline-block; flex-shrink: 0; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1; padding-inline: 0px; color: rgb(80, 82, 88);"></span></p></h3><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">SNDK最大的特點，也是最容易被忽視的風險，就是它屬於「強周期行業」，<strong>NAND Flash的價格由供需決定。</strong>需求好時，價格暴漲，供給過多時，利潤縮水，隨之價格崩跌。</p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">這跟你熟悉的台積電、蘋果等成長股不一樣，成長股靠的是業務擴張帶來的穩定增長，而周期股靠的是價格波動帶來的利潤變化。所以投資 SNDK，千萬不要抱著「長期持有、穩定獲利」的想法，而是要掌握周期的節奏。</p><h3 style="padding: 0px; margin: 1.31249em 0px 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 1.142em; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); scroll-margin-top: 48px; white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;"><span style="color: rgb(151, 72, 6);">AI帶來的需求爆發</span></h3><h3 style="padding: 0px; margin: 1.31249em 0px 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 1.142em; line-height: 1.5; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); scroll-margin-top: 48px; white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><p style="position: absolute; margin-left: 6px; opacity: 0; transition: opacity 0.2s; line-height: 1.75em;"><span class="_1e0c1o8l _vchhusvi _1o9zidpf _vwz4kb7n _y4ti1igz _bozg1mb9 _12va1onz _jcxd1r8n" style="display: inline-block; flex-shrink: 0; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1; padding-inline: 0px; color: rgb(80, 82, 88);"></span></p></h3><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">2025年到2026年，全球AI資料中心大規模建置，企業級需求爆炸性增長。在供不應求的環境下，定價權完全掌握在供應商手中，很多雲端廠商和 AI 公司開始預付1-3 年的貨款，搶佔產能。這也是近期股價上漲的主要原因。自2026年初以來，SNDK股價累計漲幅已超過<strong>300%</strong>，而2025年全年漲幅更高達<strong>580%</strong>。</p><h3 style="padding: 0px; margin: 1.31249em 0px 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 1.142em; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); scroll-margin-top: 48px; white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;"><span style="color: rgb(151, 72, 6);">市場情緒放大波動</span></h3><h3 style="padding: 0px; margin: 1.31249em 0px 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 1.142em; line-height: 1.5; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); scroll-margin-top: 48px; white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><p style="position: absolute; margin-left: 6px; opacity: 0; transition: opacity 0.2s; line-height: 1.75em;"><span class="_1e0c1o8l _vchhusvi _1o9zidpf _vwz4kb7n _y4ti1igz _bozg1mb9 _12va1onz _jcxd1r8n" style="display: inline-block; flex-shrink: 0; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1; padding-inline: 0px; color: rgb(80, 82, 88);"></span></p></h3><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">很多人忽略一件事：<strong>記憶體股容易過熱。漲的時候大家瘋狂追高，跌的時候又拼命賣出。</strong></p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">SNDK 的估值已經被市場情緒推到很高的水平。2026年2月，知名做空機構Citron Research對SNDK發起空頭襲擊，直言NAND閃存價格和需求的上漲是週期性的，而非長期趨勢，認為市場存在明顯錯配。消息一出，SNDK股價一度大跌近8%，但股價在短暫修正後，不僅迅速收復失地，更在之後創下歷史新高。這說明了SNDK當下的股價波動已不僅僅由基本面驅動，多空雙方的激烈博弈正在將波動幅度拉得更大。</p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">當市場情緒逆轉，或者供給開始增加時，SNDK 的股價很可能出現劇烈回調，就像2018 年記憶體周期頂部時那樣，很多投資人在高位套牢，幾年都解不了套。</p></div></div><div class="article-content__articleDetailCon__kmMNZ" id="617703"><div class="article-content__conP__unsXk"><div class="article-content__titleSerial__NBTps observe-item"></div><h2 class="article-content__contextP__E5lG3">SNDK投資邏輯：不是成長股，而是「AI加持的周期股」</h2></div><div class="article-content__contextC__QMEJJ"><p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">很多人只看到 SNDK 漲得好就買，其實根本沒有想清楚自己<strong>為什麼買</strong>，這樣很容易在市場波動時做出錯誤決策。</p><h3 style="padding: 0px; margin: 15px 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 1.142em; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); scroll-margin-top: 48px; white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">多頭邏輯（為什麼會漲）</h3><h3 style="padding: 0px; margin: 1.31249em 0px 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 1.142em; line-height: 1.5; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); scroll-margin-top: 48px; white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><p style="position: absolute; margin-left: 6px; opacity: 0; transition: opacity 0.2s; margin-bottom: 15px; margin-top: 15px; line-height: 1.75em;"><span class="_1e0c1o8l _vchhusvi _1o9zidpf _vwz4kb7n _y4ti1igz _bozg1mb9 _12va1onz _jcxd1r8n" style="display: inline-block; flex-shrink: 0; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1; padding-inline: 0px; color: rgb(80, 82, 88);"></span></p></h3><p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">SNDK 當前的多頭邏輯非常清晰，主要基於三個核心因素：</p><p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; line-height: 1.75em;"><strong><strong style="color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap;">✅&nbsp;</strong>AI 資料需求爆發</strong>：AI 大模型和數據中心建設帶來的儲存需求，是過去幾年的 3-8 倍，這種需求不是短期的，而是長期趨勢，至少會持續 3-5 年</p><p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; line-height: 1.75em;"><strong><strong style="color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap;">✅&nbsp;</strong>記憶體供給受限</strong>：全球主要記憶體廠商（三星、美光、SK 海力士）都把產能優先分配給利潤更高的 HBM（高頻寬記憶體），導致 NAND Flash 供給緊張，這種供需錯配短期內很難緩解</p><p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; line-height: 1.75em;"><strong><strong style="color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap;">✅&nbsp;</strong>價格上升帶動利潤</strong>：供需失衡直接推動 NAND Flash 價格連續上漲，2026 年 Q1 合約價漲幅達 55%-60%，價格上漲是記憶體公司利潤最直接的放大器，每上漲 10%，利潤可能增長 50% 以上</p><p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">如果這三個因素沒有改變，SNDK 的業績和股價很可能繼續上漲，但一旦其中任何一個因素發生變化，投資人就要提高警覺。</p><h3 style="padding: 0px; margin: 15px 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 1.142em; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); scroll-margin-top: 48px; white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">投資SNDK美股的風險</h3><h3 style="padding: 0px; margin: 1.31249em 0px 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 1.142em; line-height: 1.5; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); scroll-margin-top: 48px; white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><p style="position: absolute; margin-left: 6px; opacity: 0; transition: opacity 0.2s; margin-bottom: 15px; margin-top: 15px; line-height: 1.75em;"><span class="_1e0c1o8l _vchhusvi _1o9zidpf _vwz4kb7n _y4ti1igz _bozg1mb9 _12va1onz _jcxd1r8n" style="display: inline-block; flex-shrink: 0; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1; padding-inline: 0px; color: rgb(80, 82, 88);"></span></p></h3><ul class=" list-paddingleft-2" style="list-style-type: disc;"><li><p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;"><strong>記憶體是商品（沒有護城河）</strong>：NAND Flash 本質上是標準化商品，不同廠商的產品差異不大，價格競爭激烈，一旦供給增加，價格很容易下跌，公司利潤也會隨之縮水</p></li><li><p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;"><strong>三星等競爭者壓力</strong>：三星作為全球最大的 NAND 供應商，一旦決定擴大產能，或者降價搶市場，很容易改變行業供需格局，SanDisk 的定價權並不絕對</p></li><li><p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;"><strong>周期反轉風險</strong>：記憶體行業的「高價催生產能、產能緩解高價」規律從未改變，當價格上漲到一定程度，廠商一定會擴大產能，最終導致供過於求，價格下跌，周期逆轉</p></li><li><p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;"><strong>估值過高風險</strong>：SNDK 當前的估值已經包含了未來 2-3 年的成長預期，一旦業績不及預期，或者市場情緒逆轉，估值很可能出現大幅回調，帶動股價下跌</p></li></ul><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; line-height: 1.714; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><br></p><p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;"><strong>📌小結：</strong></p><p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">SNDK不是傳統意義上的成長股，你可以把它理解為<strong>「AI加持的周期股」</strong>。它的股價上漲有AI需求的實質支撐，但同時也帶著周期股特有的暴漲暴跌基因。</p><p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">換句話說，投資SNDK的關鍵不是看公司有多好，而是看「周期處於什麼階段」。<span style="color: rgb(151, 72, 6);">當前處於周期上升階段，價格上漲，利潤增長，適合波段操作；但當供給開始增加，價格見頂時，就要果斷獲利了結，不要戀戰。</span></p></div></div><div class="article-content__articleDetailCon__kmMNZ" id="617704"><div class="article-content__conP__unsXk"><div class="article-content__titleSerial__NBTps observe-item"></div><h2 class="article-content__contextP__E5lG3">SanDisk公司能否繼續領漲記憶體行情？</h2></div><div class="article-content__contextC__QMEJJ"><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 16px; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; white-space: pre-wrap; padding: 0px; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">Sandisk能否繼續領漲，關鍵在於兩件事：</p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 16px; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; white-space: pre-wrap; padding: 0px; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;"><strong>第一，AI需求能否持續超出預期</strong></p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 16px; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; white-space: pre-wrap; padding: 0px; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;"><strong>第二，公司能否成功簽訂多年期供應協議以平滑周期波動。</strong></p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 16px; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; white-space: pre-wrap; padding: 0px; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">短期來看，供不應求的格局仍在，漲價動能尚未衰竭。中長期來看，市場對Sandisk的定價分歧巨大，這意味著股價的波動將持續處於高位。對於波段交易者而言，這既是機會，也是風險。</p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 16px; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; white-space: pre-wrap; padding: 0px; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">但NAND本質上仍是供給驅動的商品行業，歷史上多次在高毛利階段迎來周期見頂。此外，Bernstein分析師雖然給出了高達1,250美元的目標價，但市場上24位分析師的12個月平均目標價僅為594.48美元，最低目標價甚至低至32美元，這種極端的分歧本身就說明了股價的不確定性。</p><p style="line-height: 28px; margin-bottom: 24px;"><br></p></div></div><div class="article-content__articleDetailCon__kmMNZ" id="617705"><div class="article-content__conP__unsXk"><div class="article-content__titleSerial__NBTps observe-item"></div><h2 class="article-content__contextP__E5lG3">台灣人如何買SNDK美股？</h2></div><div class="article-content__contextC__QMEJJ"><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">台灣投資人要怎麼交易SNDK 這檔美股？有哪些管道，各有什麼優缺點？</p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: href="https://www.mitrade.com/zh/insights/markets/shares/SNDK" target="_blank">SNDK.US</a>），會更靈活，也更符合SNDK 的周期股屬性。</p><h3 style="padding: 0px; margin: 1.31249em 0px 0px; font-variant: normal; scroll-margin-top: 48px; white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">Mitrade 平台交易 SNDK 的優勢</h3><h3 style="padding: 0px; margin: 1.31249em 0px 0px; font-variant: font-size: 1.142em; line-height: 1.5; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, line-height: 1.75em;"><strong style="font-family: sans-serif;">✅&nbsp;操作簡單</strong><span style="font-family: sans-serif;">：註冊只要1分鐘，手機APP和電腦端都能交易，介面直覺，新手也能快速上手</span></p><p style="margin: 15px 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; line-height: 1.75em;">在平台搜尋「SNDK」或「Sandisk」</p></li><li><p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; line-height: 1.75em;">根據自己的判斷，選擇買入或賣出，設定<strong>停損和停利</strong></p></li><li><p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; line-height: 1.75em;">等待市場走勢符合預期，獲利了結</p></li></ol><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;"><em>*CFD 交易屬於高風險投資產品，槓桿交易可能導致虧損超過初始投資金額，建議先用模擬帳戶練習，熟悉操作後再小資金實盤交易。</em></p><p style="margin: 0.75em font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; line-height: 1.714; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, class="article-content__articleDetailCon__kmMNZ" id="617706"><div class="article-content__conP__unsXk"><div class="article-content__titleSerial__NBTps observe-item"></div><h2 class="article-content__contextP__E5lG3">SNDK vs WDC vs MU比較：誰更值得關注？</h2></div><div class="article-content__contextC__QMEJJ"><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">很多人會把 SNDK 跟它的母公司 Western Digital（WDC）和競爭對手美光科技（MU）放在一起比較，想知道哪一檔更值得投資。</p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">這裡我做一個簡單的比較，幫你做出更合適的選擇。</p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1.75em;">高容量儲存需求穩定、估值相對合理</p></td></tr></tbody></table></div></div></div><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; line-height: 1.714; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><br></p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">三者的選擇，取決於你看好哪個細分市場。</p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;"><strong>Micron代表的是「算力本身」</strong>。AI模型越做越大，訓練與推論都需要大量高速記憶體，特別是HBM這類高頻寬產品，幾乎已經變成AI伺服器的標配。</p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;"><strong>SanDisk所代表的是「資料如何被快速存取</strong>」。AI不只是算，還會產生海量資料，這些資料需要被即時寫入、讀取、再利用。它決定了整個系統的流暢度與效率。也因為這樣，SanDisk的成長往往帶著更強的景氣循環特性，當需求爆發時，它會跑得很快；但一旦庫存或價格反轉，波動也會特別明顯。</p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">最後是<strong>Western Digital，它更接近「資料最終會流向哪裡」</strong>。當AI產生的資料被整理、沉澱，最終還是需要一個低成本、大容量的地方長期存放，這就是HDD存在的價值。雖然成長速度不如前兩者，但勝在需求穩定，而且與大型雲端與資料中心高度綁定。換句話說，它不是在賺AI爆發的第一波，而是在吃長期資料累積的尾端紅利。</p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; line-height: 1.714; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><br></p></div></div><div class="article-content__articleDetailCon__kmMNZ" id="617707"><div class="article-content__conP__unsXk"><div class="article-content__titleSerial__NBTps observe-item"></div><h2 class="article-content__contextP__E5lG3">結論：SNDK的核心投資邏輯</h2></div><div class="article-content__contextC__QMEJJ"><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">回頭看我們討論的所有內容。SNDK本質上是一家<strong>受AI需求驅動的NAND Flash記憶體公司</strong>。它的股價暴漲有紮實的基本面支撐——AI資料中心需求爆發、供給受限、價格持續上漲。但它同時也帶著記憶體產業特有的<strong>週期性風險</strong>。</p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">這檔股票不適合長期持有型投資人。它更適合那些<strong>願意持續追蹤供需變化、能夠承受較大波動、並且有明確進出場紀律的交易者</strong>。</p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">記住，<strong>在NAND價格上漲周期布局，見頂時賣出，賺取波段收益。</strong>每次交易設定 5%-10% 的止損，避免在市場劇烈波動時出現大幅虧損。</p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">另外，建議先用Mitrade 的免費模擬帳戶測試，熟悉SNDK的波動節奏和交易操作，再進入實盤交易，這樣能有效降低風險。</p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;">👉 <a href="https://mytd.cc/u4vU" target="_blank">立即開設 Mitrade 模擬賬戶，免費開始交易</a></p></div></div><div class="article-faq__faq__uFyje"><div class="article-faq__faqTit__59aJp">常見問題</div><div><div class="article-faq__faqItem__n9HJz"><div class="article-faq__title__7XhjR"><h3>SNDK 納入納斯達克 100 指數，對股價有什麼影響？</h3><i class="iconfont icon-more"></i></div><div class="article-faq__desc__wNHkv "><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.714; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; white-space: pre-wrap; padding: 0px; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">納入納斯達克 100 指數對 SNDK 是利好，主要有兩個影響：</p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; line-height: 1.714;"><strong>被動資金流入</strong>：跟蹤納斯達克 100 指數的 ETF（如 QQQ）會被動買入 SNDK，帶來數十億美元的被動資金流入。</p><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; line-height: 1.714;"><strong>市場認可度提升</strong>：納入納斯達克 100 代表 SNDK 的規模和流動性達到標準，會吸引更多機構投資者買入，提升市場認可度</p><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.714; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; white-space: pre-wrap; padding: 0px; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">不過要注意，納入指數前後，股價可能會有「買預期、賣事實」的行情，投資人要避免在納入前追高，以免在納入後出現回調時被套。</p></div></div><div class="article-faq__faqItem__n9HJz"><div class="article-faq__title__7XhjR"><h3>SNDK的財報該看哪些重點，才能判斷公司好不好？</h3><i class="iconfont icon-more"></i></div><div class="article-faq__desc__wNHkv "><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.714; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; white-space: pre-wrap; padding: 0px; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">SNDK 作為周期股，財報重點跟成長股不一樣，核心看三個指標：</p><ol class="ak-ol list-paddingleft-2" style="margin: 10px 0px 0px; width: 1584.58px; padding: 0px 0px 0px 24px; white-space: pre-wrap; box-sizing: border-box; display: flow-root; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><li><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; line-height: 1.714;"><strong>企業級 SSD 收入占比</strong>：這是衡量 AI 業務滲透率的關鍵，占比越高越好</p></li><li><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; line-height: 1.714;"><strong>毛利率</strong>：NAND 價格上漲時，毛利率會明顯提升，這是利潤增長的核心驅動力</p></li><li><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; line-height: 1.714;"><strong>訂單可見度</strong>：看公司的訂單是否排到未來 1-3 年，客戶是否預付貨款，這能反映市場需求的強勁程度。</p></li></ol></div></div><div class="article-faq__faqItem__n9HJz"><div class="article-faq__title__7XhjR"><h3>台灣投資人交易 SNDK，需要注意哪些稅務問題？</h3><i class="iconfont icon-more"></i></div><div class="article-faq__desc__wNHkv "><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.714; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; white-space: pre-wrap; padding: 0px; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">台灣投資人交易美股需要注意兩個稅務問題：</p><ol class="ak-ol list-paddingleft-2" style="margin: 10px 0px 0px; width: 1584.58px; padding: 0px 0px 0px 24px; white-space: pre-wrap; box-sizing: border-box; display: flow-root; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><li><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; line-height: 1.714;"><strong>股息稅</strong>：如果持有 SNDK 股票獲得分紅，美國會預扣 30% 的股息稅，台灣跟美國有租稅協定，可以申請退稅，實際稅率 15%</p></li><li><p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; line-height: 1.714;"><strong>資本利得稅</strong>：台灣投資人賣出美股獲得的資本利得，需要申報台灣的綜合所得稅，按個人所得稅率課稅</p></li></ol><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.714; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; white-space: pre-wrap; padding: 0px; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">如果透過 Mitrade交易 SNDK CFD，因為不需要實際持有股票，所以不需要考慮股息稅，只有資本利得需要申報，相對簡單很多。</p></div></div><div class="article-faq__faqItem__n9HJz"><div class="article-faq__title__7XhjR"><h3>SNDK現在還能買嗎？</h3><i class="iconfont icon-more"></i></div><div class="article-faq__desc__wNHkv "><p style="margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: normal; font-kerning: auto; font-optical-sizing: auto; font-feature-settings: normal; font-variation-settings: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.714; font-family: &quot;Atlassian Sans&quot;, ui-sans-serif, -apple-system, &quot;system-ui&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Ubuntu, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; white-space: pre-wrap; padding: 0px; color: rgb(41, 42, 46); background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">這取決於你的交易週期和風險承受能力。SNDK當前的股價已經反映了相當樂觀的預期，短期波動風險較高。如果你是波段交易者，建議先用模擬賬戶測試策略；如果你是長期投資者，需要仔細評估自己能否承受記憶體週期反轉時的大幅回調。</p></div></div></div></div><div class="article-content__affirms__QFojR"><p><span style="font-size: 14px;"><em>* 本文內容僅代表作者個人觀點，讀者不應以本文作為任何投資依據。在做出任何投資決定之前，您應該尋求獨立財務顧問的建議，以確保您了解風險。</em><em>差價合約（CFD）是槓桿性產品，有可能導致您損失全部資金。這些產品並不適合所有人，請謹慎投資。</em></span><a href="https://www.mitrade.com/docs/Mitrade_RiskDisclosureStatement-zh-TW.pdf" target="_blank" style="font-size: 14px;"><em>查閱詳情</em></a><br/></p><p><br/></p></div></div><div pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;\"\u003E白話解釋一下，你每天用的手機記憶卡、筆電裡的 SSD 固態硬碟、USB 隨身碟，還有雲端資料中心裡用來儲存大量數據的設備，很多都是用 SanDisk 的 NAND Flash 技術製造的。你可以把它想成是數位世界的「倉庫管理員」，負責把所有數據妥善儲存起來，需要的時候再快速取出。\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Ch3 style=\"padding: 0px; margin: 1.31249em 0px 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: none; font-language-override: \u003Cstrong\u003E消費電子\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E：手機、電腦、數位相機等，這是 SanDisk 的傳統強項，也是大家最熟悉的業務。比如手機裡的內置儲存、替換用的記憶卡，筆電的 SSD 硬碟等，屬於穩定現金流業務，利潤率中等。\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp style=\"margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; rgb(41, 42, 46); white-space: pre-wrap; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;\"\u003E2️⃣ \u003Cstrong\u003E企業\u002F資料中心\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E：雲端服務、AI 伺服器。這是2026年增長最快的業務，也是 SNDK 跟 AI 最直接相關的部分。AI 大模型訓練需要處理 PB 級的數據，一臺AI 伺服器對 NAND 儲存的需求是傳統伺服器的 3-8 倍，這種爆發性需求直接推動了公司業績增長。\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp style=\"margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant: normal; font-size-adjust: rgb(255, 255, 255); line-height: 1.75em;\"\u003E3️⃣ \u003Cstrong\u003E工業與車用\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E：自動駕駛、邊緣運算設備的儲存需求。這部分業務規模相對小，但增長穩定。\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp style=\"margin: 0.75em 0px 0px; 時代的基礎設施供應商」。\u003C\u002Fspan\u003EAI 需要大量算力，更需要大量儲存空間，沒有足夠的 NAND Flash，再強大的 AI 模型也無法運轉。這也是為什麼 SNDK能在 AI浪潮中脫穎而出的關鍵原因。\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Ch3 style=\"padding: 0px; margin: 1.31249em 0px 0px;
